Coaches program 12-week strength plans, track client form, and send notes. Users log sets, view progress, and get automatically guided to their next session. The product is pre-scaffold but not yet feature-complete — agents are building it batch by batch via the `/monitor/roadmap` kickoff system.\n    17→\n    18→## Data Flow\n    19→\n    20→```\n    21→Browser ──► proxy.ts (auth guard + PIN gate + Supabase session refresh)\n    22→         ──► App Router server components (lib/supabase/server.ts)\n    23→         ──► Supabase PostgreSQL (RLS enforced)\n    24→\n    25→Monitor ──► /monitor/roadmap (server component, reads GitHub PR status + Upstash KV)\n    26→         ──► KickoffButton → POST /api/monitor/kickoff\n    27→         ──► GitHub workflow_dispatch → claude-feature.yml\n    28→         ──► Claude Code agent (reads GitHub Issue for spec, writes code, commits, pushes)\n    29→         ──► PR marked ready → human reviews + merges\n    30→```\n    31→\n    32→## Tech Stack\n    33→\n    34→| Layer | Technology |\n    35→|---|---|\n    36→| Framework | Next.js 16.2.2 — App Router, `proxy.ts` (not `middleware.ts`) |\n    37→| UI | React 19, Tailwind v4 (CSS-first), shadcn/ui v4 (base-nova style) |\n    38→| Auth + DB | Supabase (PostgreSQL + RLS + SSR auth via `@supabase/ssr`) |\n    39→| KV store | Upstash Redis (`@upstash/redis`) — roadmap status overrides only |\n    40→| Charts | Recharts |\n    41→| Animation | Framer Motion |\n    42→| DnD | dnd-kit (Batch 7) |\n    43→| Toast | Sonner |\n    44→| Server state | TanStack React Query |\n    45→| Client state | Zustand |\n    46→| Tests | Vitest + jsdom |\n    47→| CI | GitHub Actions — `claude-feature.yml` (agent) + `ci.yml` (lint/test) |\n    48→| Hosting | Vercel (auto-deploy `main`; preview on all branches) |\n    49→| Package mgr | pnpm 9 |\n    50→\n    51→## Key Files\n    52→\n    53→| File | Purpose |\n    54→|---|---|\n    55→| `proxy.ts` | Auth guard + monitor PIN gate + Supabase session refresh. {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01AA4DfoW1mm6RftthXKhe5j","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→---\n     2→type: gotchas\n     3→tags: [gotchas, lessons-learned, buildbase]\n     4→last-updated: 2026-04-16\n     5→---\n     6→\n     7→# Gotchas — BuildBase\n     8→\n     9→> Read this before starting any task. Each entry is a real thing that burned us.\n    10→> Add new entries at the top with the date.\n    11→\n    12→---\n    13→\n    14→## 2026-04-24 — Test files with JSX must use .tsx extension\n    15→\n    16→**Symptom:** `pnpm tsc --noEmit` fails with dozens of `'>' expected`, `',' expected`, and `Expression expected` errors in test files.\n    17→\n    18→**Cause:** TypeScript cannot parse JSX syntax (`<Component />`) in `.ts` files. The file must have a `.tsx` extension for JSX to be valid. This has burned us on items 3-2 and 3-3 — both times the agent wrote React component render tests in a `.ts` file.\n    19→\n    20→**Rule for test files:**\n    21→- If a test **imports and renders React components** (uses `render()`, JSX, `screen.*`) → name it `*.test.tsx`\n    22→- If a test **only tests pure functions, data transforms, and logic** (no JSX) → name it `*.test.ts`\n    23→\n    24→Most BuildBase tests should be `.test.ts` because coverage targets `lib/**/*.ts` (pure logic). Prefer testing the logic the component uses, not rendering the component itself. Only write `.tsx` tests when you specifically need to test interactive UI behavior.\n    25→\n    26→---\n    27→\n    28→## 2026-04-16 — TypeScript strict mode: never initialize array/object state with null\n    29→\n    30→**Symptom:** `pnpm tsc --noEmit` fails with `Type 'null' is not assignable to type 'OptimisticSet'` (or similar). Commit step is blocked, PR ends up with 0 files changed.\n    31→\n    32→**Cause:** `strictNullChecks` is on. `useState<T>(null)` is only valid if the type is `T | null`. Initializing array state with `null` instead of `[]` causes a hard TS error.\n    33→\n    34→**Fix:**\n    35→```ts\n    36→// WRONG — TS2322 in strict mode\n    37→const [sets, setSets] = useState<OptimisticSet[]>(null)\n    38→const [item, setItem] = useState<SetLog>(null)\n    39→\n    40→// CORRECT\n    41→const [sets, setSets] = useState<OptimisticSet[]>([])\n    42→const [item, setItem] = useState<SetLog | null>(null)\n    43→```\n    44→When null IS a valid value, add `| null` to the type. When it's an empty collection, start with `[]`.\n    45→\n    46→---\n    47→\n    48→## 2026-04-16 — claude-code-action@beta requires `mode: agent` + `direct_prompt`\n    49→\n    50→**Symptom:** Workflow run fails immediately with:\n    51→`Error: Prepare step failed with error: Tag mode cannot handle workflow_dispatch events. Use 'agent' mode for automation events.`\n    52→\n    53→**Cause:** `claude-code-action@beta` changed its API. The old input `prompt:` is no longer valid — it must be `direct_prompt:`. And `workflow_dispatch` events require `mode: agent` to be set explicitly (default mode is \"tag\" which only works on PR/issue events).\n    54→\n    55→**Fix:**\n    56→```yaml\n    57→- uses: anthropics/claude-code-action@beta\n    58→  with:\n    59→    anthropic_api_key: ${{ secrets.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY }}\n    60→    mode: agent          # ← required for workflow_dispatch\n    61→    direct_prompt: |     # ← not \"prompt:\"\n    62→      ...\n    63→```\n    64→\n    65→---\n    66→\n    67→## 2026-04-16 — ANTHROPIC_API_KEY must be in GitHub Actions secrets (not just Vercel)\n    68→\n    69→**Symptom:** After fixing the mode error, workflow fails with:\n    70→`Error: Environment variable validation failed: Either ANTHROPIC_API_KEY or CLAUDE_CODE_OAUTH_TOKEN is required when using direct Anthropic API.`\n    71→\n    72→**Cause:** `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` is set as a Vercel env var (for any future server-side AI use) but GitHub Actions has its own separate secrets store. The workflow's `secrets.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` looks in the repo's Actions secrets, not Vercel.\n    73→\n    74→**Fix:** Go to GitHub → repo → Settings → Secrets and variables → Actions → New repository secret → `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`.\n    75→\n    76→---\n    77→\n    78→## 2026-04-16 — GitHub workflow file: merge conflicts silently drop critical lines\n    79→\n    80→**Symptom:** PR was merged, but `mode: agent` and `direct_prompt:` still weren't on main. The old `prompt:` key survived.\n    81→\n    82→**Cause:** When multiple PRs touched `.github/workflows/claude-feature.yml`, the merge conflict was resolved back to the old version. GitHub's merge commit silently kept the old field names.\n    83→\n    84→**Fix:** After any PR touching `claude-feature.yml`, always verify with `git show origin/main:.github/workflows/claude-feature.yml | grep -E \"mode:|direct_prompt:|prompt:\"` before triggering a kickoff.\n    85→\n    86→---\n    87→\n    88→## 2026-04-16 — Issue numbers must be stamped in roadmap-data.ts before kickoff\n    89→\n    90→**Symptom:** Clicking \"Start\" creates a new duplicate GitHub Issue every time, even when the issue already exists.\n    91→\n    92→**Cause:** `createIssue()` is guarded by `item.issue ?? existing?.issue ?? null`. If `item.issue` is `undefined` in `roadmap-data.ts` AND Upstash Redis is not configured (so `existing` is always `{}`), the guard fails and a new issue is created unconditionally on every click.\n    93→\n    94→**Fix:** All issue numbers are now stamped in `lib/roadmap-data.ts` (items 1-1 through 7-3 → GitHub issues #17–40). Never remove these numbers. Duplicate issues #42–44, #47 were closed.\n    95→\n    96→---\n    97→\n    98→## 2026-04-16 — Workflow commit step silently succeeds with 0 changes\n    99→\n   100→**Symptom:** PR is marked \"ready for review\" but has 0 file changes — only the empty init commit.\n   101→\n   102→**Cause:** The commit step had `|| echo \"Nothing to commit\"` which swallowed the git failure. Then `git push` pushed the empty branch and `gh pr ready` marked it done. The Claude Code agent may have written nothing (model/auth issue) but the workflow appeared to succeed.\n   103→\n   104→**Fix:** Added a \"Verify changes exist\" step before commit:\n   105→```bash\n   106→git add -A\n   107→if git diff --cached --quiet; then\n   108→  echo \"::error::Claude Code produced no file changes.\"\n   109→  exit 1\n   110→fi\n   111→```\n   112→\n   113→---\n   114→\n   115→## 2026-04-15 — GitHub fine-grained PAT needs 4 specific permissions\n   116→\n   117→**Symptom:** `/api/monitor/kickoff` returns `{ \"error\": \"Failed to prepare branch — check GITHUB_TOKEN permissions\" }`.\n   118→\n   119→**Cause:** The fine-grained PAT used as `GITHUB_TOKEN` in Vercel was missing one or more required permissions.\n   120→\n   121→**Required permissions (all must be Read and write):**\n   122→- **Contents** — create branches, create commits via git data API\n   123→- **Pull requests** — create draft PRs\n   124→- **Issues** — create/read GitHub Issues\n   125→- **Actions** — trigger `workflow_dispatch`\n   126→\n   127→---\n   128→\n   129→## 2026-04-15 — Branch must have ≥1 commit ahead of main for PR creation\n   130→\n   131→**Symptom:** `createDraftPr()` returns 422 from GitHub: \"No commits between main and feat/...\".\n   132→\n   133→**Cause:** GitHub requires the head branch to have at least one commit that main doesn't have before a PR can be created. `createBranch()` alone just creates a ref pointing to the same SHA as main — same tree, no diff.\n   134→\n   135→**Fix:** `ensureBranchReady()` in `lib/github-api.ts` calls `createEmptyCommit()` when the branch HEAD SHA equals main's HEAD SHA. This creates a git commit with the same tree but a new hash, satisfying GitHub's requirement.\n   136→\n   137→---\n   138→\n   139→## 2026-04-15 — Upstash Redis env vars required for live in-progress status\n   140→\n   141→**Symptom:** Clicking \"Start\" fires the kickoff API, button shows \"Started → PR\", but the roadmap page never updates to show \"In Progress\" after `router.refresh()`.\n   142→\n   143→**Cause:** `setRoadmapOverride()` in `lib/storage.ts` silently no-ops if `UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL` / `UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN` are not set. The KV write is skipped, so on the next page render the static `roadmap-data.ts` status (not-started) is still shown.\n   144→\n   145→**Fix:** Set both Upstash env vars in Vercel. The monitor degrades gracefully without them but live status updates don't work.\n   146→\n   147→---\n   148→\n   149→## Next.js 16 — proxy.ts replaces middleware.ts\n   150→\n   151→**Symptom:** Auth guard or session refresh logic silently does nothing.\n   152→\n   153→**Cause:** Next.js 16 renamed `middleware.ts` → `proxy.ts`. The exported function must be named `proxy`, not `middleware`. A `middleware.ts` at the root is silently ignored.\n   154→\n   155→**Fix:**\n   156→```ts\n   157→// CORRECT — proxy.ts\n   158→export async function proxy(request: NextRequest) { ... }\n   159→export const config = { matcher: [...] }; // no `runtime` key — build error\n   160→\n   161→// WRONG — silently no-ops\n   162→export function middleware(request: NextRequest) { ... }\n   163→```\n   164→Note: `runtime` is not allowed in proxy.ts config — it always runs on Node.js.\n   165→\n   166→---\n   167→\n   168→## Next.js 16 — params and cookies/headers are async\n   169→\n   170→**Symptom:** `params.id` is undefined; `cookies()` causes a type error.\n   171→\n   172→**Fix:**\n   173→```ts\n   174→// Pages/layouts\n   175→export default async function Page({ params }: { params: Promise<{ id: string }> }) {\n   176→  const { id } = await params;\n   177→}\n   178→\n   179→// Server components\n   180→const cookieStore = await cookies();\n   181→const headersList = await headers();\n   182→```\n   183→\n   184→---\n   185→\n   186→## Tailwind v4 — no tailwind.config.ts, @theme is CSS-first\n   187→\n   188→**Symptom:** Custom tokens not resolving, or shadcn init breaks fonts.\n   189→\n   190→**Cause:** Tailwind v4 uses CSS-first config. All design tokens live in the `@theme {}` block in `app/globals.css`. Font references inside `@theme` must be literal strings — `var()` references resolve at parse time and can't see Next.js runtime injections.\n   191→\n   192→**Fix:**\n   193→```css\n   194→/* CORRECT */\n   195→--font-sans: \"Inter\", ui-sans-serif, system-ui, sans-serif;\n   196→\n   197→/* WRONG — circular */\n   198→--font-sans: var(--font-sans);\n   199→\n   200→/* WRONG — next/font injects this at runtime, @theme can't see it */\n   201→--font-sans: var(--font-inter);\n   202→```\n   203→\n   204→---\n   205→\n   206→## Supabase — getUser() not getSession() in proxy.ts\n   207→\n   208→**Symptom:** Auth seems to work but sessions don't refresh correctly; stale tokens.\n   209→\n   210→**Cause:** `getSession()` reads from the cookie without re-validating against the Supabase auth server. Only `getUser()` re-validates and refreshes the session token.\n   211→\n   212→**Fix:** `proxy.ts` must use `supabase.auth.getUser()`.\n   213→\n   214→---\n   215→\n   216→## Supabase — coach_form_assessments is coach-only, forever\n   217→\n   218→**Symptom:** Form assessment scores visible to users in the UI.\n   219→\n   220→**Cause:** The `coach_form_assessments` table was queried in a user-facing component.\n   221→\n   222→**Fix:** Users NEVER see raw form status. Use `getFormBadge(status)` from `lib/utils.ts`:\n   223→- `locked_in` → `\"Solid Form ✅\"`\n   224→- Everything else → `null`\n   225→RLS on the table also enforces this at the DB level.\n   226→\n   227→---\n   228→\n   229→## Monitor — MONITOR_COOKIE name is the source of truth\n   230→\n   231→The monitor cookie name is `_bb_ok`, defined in `lib/constants.ts` as `MONITOR_COOKIE`. Both `proxy.ts` and `/api/monitor/kickoff/route.ts` parse the raw `Cookie` header for this value. If the name ever changes, update both files.\n   232→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it looks malicious. {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_011SHYB48yrsecNgzKbj1QX7","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→# BuildBase — Design System\n     2→\n     3→This document is the visual and interaction contract for every agent and developer building features. Read it before writing any UI. **Non-negotiable** items are marked ⛔.\n     4→\n     5→---\n     6→\n     7→## 1. Visual Identity\n     8→\n     9→BuildBase is a **warm, parchment-toned, athletic** application. The visual language should feel like a sunlit training journal — purposeful, high-contrast brown-on-cream, built for performance, not for decoration. No dark mode. No heavy drop-shadows. No glassmorphism. Forest green and burnt orange are accent colors only, not primary surfaces.\n    10→\n    11→The brand is the combination of two distinct elements:\n    12→- **Build** — deep forest green `#1C3A2A`. Steady. Structural.\n    13→- **Base** — burnt orange `#C84B1A`. Action. Energy.\n    14→\n    15→```tsx\n    16→// ⛔ MUST use this exact treatment everywhere the name appears\n    17→<span style={{ color: \"#1C3A2A\" }}>Build</span>\n    18→<span style={{ color: \"#C84B1A\", fontWeight: 700 }}>Base</span>\n    19→```\n    20→\n    21→---\n    22→\n    23→## 2. Color System\n    24→\n    25→### Surfaces (backgrounds — 4 levels)\n    26→\n    27→| Token | Hex | Use when |\n    28→|-------|-----|---------|\n    29→| `--color-bg-base` | `#EDE4D3` | Page backgrounds, the \"floor\" (warm parchment) |\n    30→| `--color-bg-surface` | `#E5DAC8` | Sidebar, sticky headers, nav |\n    31→| `--color-bg-elevated` | `#E8DECE` | Cards, panels, inputs |\n    32→| `--color-bg-hover` | `#DDD2BF` | Hover states on clickable surfaces |\n    33→\n    34→⛔ Never go more than one level of elevation in a single card stack. A card inside a card inside a card creates visual mud.\n    35→\n    36→### Content (text)\n    37→\n    38→| Token | Hex | Use when |\n    39→|-------|-----|---------|\n    40→| `--color-content-primary` | `#2C1A10` | Headings, primary body text (deep brown) |\n    41→| `--color-content-secondary` | `#6B5A48` | Supporting copy, labels, subtitles (warm brown) |\n    42→| `--color-content-muted` | `#988A78` | Timestamps, metadata, disabled text (soft brown) |\n    43→\n    44→### Borders\n    45→\n    46→| Token | Hex | Use when |\n    47→|-------|-----|---------|\n    48→| `--color-border-subtle` | `#C8B99D` | Default card borders, dividers |\n    49→| `--color-border-strong` | `#B5A68C` | Focus rings, active states |\n    50→\n    51→### Accent and Brand\n    52→\n    53→| Token | Hex | Use when |\n    54→|-------|-----|---------|\n    55→| `--color-accent` | `#C84B1A` | CTAs, active nav indicator, badges |\n    56→| `--color-accent-dim` | `#8C3410` | Hover state of accent elements, bar/rod in logo |\n    57→| `--color-brand` | `#1C3A2A` | \"Build\" text, decorative brand moments |\n    58→\n    59→### Semantic\n    60→\n    61→| Token | Hex | Use when |\n    62→|-------|-----|---------|\n    63→| `--color-success` | `#2D7A3A` | Completed sessions, set logged confirmation |\n    64→| `--color-warning` | `#C08030` | CI pending, soreness alert |\n    65→| `--color-error` | `#B83020` | Auth errors, CI failure |\n    66→| `--color-info` | `#3060A0` | In-progress badges, PR links |\n    67→\n    68→### Effort Scale (1–5)\n    69→\n    70→```\n    71→1 → #D32F2F  🔴 (Easy / didn't even try)\n    72→2 → #F57C00  🟠\n    73→3 → #FBC02D  🟡\n    74→4 → #388E3C  🟢\n    75→5 → #1B5E20  💚 (Maxed out)\n    76→```\n    77→\n    78→---\n    79→\n    80→## 3. Typography\n    81→\n    82→Two typefaces. That's it.\n    83→\n    84→| Role | Family | When |\n    85→|------|--------|------|\n    86→| `--font-display` | Space Grotesk | Page titles, section headings, logo, numbers in stats |\n    87→| `--font-sans` | Inter | All body text, labels, buttons, nav |\n    88→\n    89→### Scale\n    90→\n    91→```\n    92→Page title (h1):    font-display, 22–28px, weight 700\n    93→Section heading:    font-display, 16–18px, weight 700\n    94→Card heading:       font-display, 14–15px, weight 600\n    95→Body:               font-sans,    14–15px, weight 400–500\n    96→Label / caption:    font-sans,    12–13px, weight 500\n    97→Metadata / mono:    font-mono,    11–12px, weight 400\n    98→```\n    99→\n   100→⛔ Never use font-display for body copy — it becomes unreadable at small sizes and lengths.\n   101→⛔ Never use `text-transform: uppercase` on body text. It's acceptable only for short status badges (<3 words).\n   102→\n   103→### Line heights\n   104→\n   105→- Headings: 1.2–1.3\n   106→- Body: 1.5–1.6\n   107→- Labels/metadata: 1.4\n   108→\n   109→---\n   110→\n   111→## 4. Spacing & Density\n   112→\n   113→BuildBase uses **comfortable density** throughout: enough breathing room that the UI feels premium, tight enough that information isn't spread thin.\n   114→\n   115→### Core rhythm: 4px grid\n   116→\n   117→Every spacing value should be a multiple of 4px. Common values:\n   118→- `4px` — internal padding on tiny badges\n   119→- `8px` — gap between icon and label\n   120→- `12px` — inner card padding (compact)\n   121→- `16px` — default card padding, section gap\n   122→- `24px` — between cards/sections\n   123→- `32px` — page-level vertical spacing\n   124→- `48px` — large section separators\n   125→\n   126→### Page layout\n   127→\n   128→```\n   129→Max content width: 1200px (centered)\n   130→Page horizontal padding: 16px mobile / 24px tablet / 32px desktop\n   131→Sidebar width: 220px (fixed, left)\n   132→Main content: 100% - 220px on lg+\n   133→```\n   134→\n   135→---\n   136→\n   137→## 5. Component Patterns\n   138→\n   139→### Cards\n   140→\n   141→The primary container for all content. Three variants:\n   142→\n   143→```\n   144→Default:\n   145→  background: #E8DECE\n   146→  border: 1px solid #C8B99D\n   147→  border-radius: 12px\n   148→  padding: 20px\n   149→\n   150→Elevated (floating dialog, etc.):\n   151→  background: #E5DAC8\n   152→  border: 1px solid #B5A68C\n   153→  border-radius: 12px\n   154→  box-shadow: 0 2px 12px rgba(0,0,0,0.06)\n   155→\n   156→Accent-edge (current session, CTA focus):\n   157→  same as Default but with:\n   158→  border-left: 3px solid #C84B1A\n   159→```\n   160→\n   161→⛔ Don't nest Default cards inside Default cards. Use Elevated for inner containers.\n   162→\n   163→### Buttons\n   164→\n   165→```\n   166→Primary (CTA):\n   167→  background: #C84B1A\n   168→  color: #FEFCF8\n   169→  font-weight: 600\n   170→  border-radius: 8px\n   171→  padding: 11px 20px\n   172→  no border\n   173→  hover: background #D95520, transform scale(1.01)\n   174→  active: transform scale(0.99)\n   175→  disabled: opacity 0.4, cursor not-allowed\n   176→\n   177→Secondary:\n   178→  background: transparent\n   179→  border: 1px solid #B5A68C\n   180→  color: #6B5A48\n   181→  hover: background #DDD2BF, border-color #C84B1A, color #2C1A10\n   182→\n   183→Ghost:\n   184→  background: transparent\n   185→  color: #6B5A48\n   186→  no border\n   187→  hover: color #2C1A10, background rgba(0,0,0,0.04)\n   188→\n   189→Destructive:\n   190→  background: rgba(184,48,32,0.12)\n   191→  border: 1px solid rgba(184,48,32,0.3)\n   192→  color: #B83020\n   193→  hover: background rgba(184,48,32,0.2)\n   194→```\n   195→\n   196→### Inputs\n   197→\n   198→```\n   199→background: #EDE4D3\n   200→border: 1px solid #C8B99D\n   201→border-radius: 8px\n   202→padding: 11px 14px\n   203→font-size: 15px\n   204→color: #2C1A10\n   205→placeholder: #988A78\n   206→transition: border-color 0.15s\n   207→\n   208→:focus → border-color: #C84B1A, outline: none\n   209→:invalid/:error → border-color: #B83020\n   210→```\n   211→\n   212→⛔ Always use `type=\"password\"` with a show/hide toggle for password fields. Never leave a bare password input.\n   213→⛔ Always pair inputs with a visible `<label>`. No placeholder-only labels.\n   214→\n   215→### Badges / Status chips\n   216→\n   217→```\n   218→Compact pill: padding 2px 8px, border-radius 6px, font-size 11px, font-weight 700\n   219→Full chip: padding 4px 12px, border-radius 8px, font-size 12px, font-weight 600\n   220→\n   221→Status colors follow semantic tokens:\n   222→  not-started: border-subtle background\n   223→  in-progress: info (#3060A0) with 10% opacity background\n   224→  done: success (#2D7A3A) with 10% opacity background\n   225→  paused: secondary text, muted background\n   226→```\n   227→\n   228→### Navigation (Sidebar)\n   229→\n   230→```\n   231→Active item:\n   232→  background: rgba(200,75,26,0.1)\n   233→  border-left: 3px solid #C84B1A\n   234→  color: #2C1A10\n   235→  icon: accent color\n   236→\n   237→Inactive item:\n   238→  background: transparent\n   239→  color: #6B5A48\n   240→  icon: muted color\n   241→  hover: background #DDD2BF, color #2C1A10\n   242→```\n   243→\n   244→---\n   245→\n   246→## 6. Chart Design (Recharts)\n   247→\n   248→### Color palette for data series\n   249→\n   250→When multiple series are shown, use this order:\n   251→```\n   252→Series 1: #C84B1A  (accent/primary)\n   253→Series 2: #2D7A3A  (success/green)\n   254→Series 3: #3060A0  (info/blue)\n   255→Series 4: #C08030  (warning/amber)\n   256→Series 5: #6B5A48  (secondary/muted)\n   257→```\n   258→\n   259→### Line charts (progress per lift)\n   260→\n   261→```tsx\n   262→// Recharts config — use these exact values\n   263→<LineChart>\n   264→  <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray=\"3 3\" stroke=\"#C8B99D\" vertical={false} />\n   265→  <XAxis\n   266→    tick={{ fill: \"#988A78\", fontSize: 11 }}\n   267→    axisLine={{ stroke: \"#C8B99D\" }}\n   268→    tickLine={false}\n   269→  />\n   270→  <YAxis\n   271→    tick={{ fill: \"#988A78\", fontSize: 11 }}\n   272→    axisLine={false}\n   273→    tickLine={false}\n   274→    width={40}\n   275→  />\n   276→  <Tooltip\n   277→    contentStyle={{\n   278→      background: \"#E8DECE\",\n   279→      border: \"1px solid #C8B99D\",\n   280→      borderRadius: 8,\n   281→      color: \"#2C1A10\",\n   282→      fontSize: 13,\n   283→    }}\n   284→    cursor={{ stroke: \"#B5A68C\", strokeDasharray: \"4 4\" }}\n   285→  />\n   286→  <Line\n   287→    type=\"monotone\"\n   288→    strokeWidth={2}\n   289→    dot={false}\n   290→    activeDot={{ r: 5, fill: \"#C84B1A\", strokeWidth: 0 }}\n   291→  />\n   292→</LineChart>\n   293→```\n   294→\n   295→### General charting rules\n   296→\n   297→- ⛔ No chart borders on the chart container itself (the card provides the border)\n   298→- ⛔ No chart titles inside the SVG — put them above in the card header\n   299→- Remove unnecessary grid lines. Horizontal gridlines only.\n   300→- Tooltip should always show the exact value + unit (e.g., \"135 lbs\")\n   301→- When showing effort/soreness, use the effort scale colors from §2\n   302→- Keep chart height between 200–320px for embedded charts, 400px for full-page\n   303→\n   304→---\n   305→\n   306→## 7. Motion & Animation (framer-motion)\n   307→\n   308→### Principles\n   309→\n   310→1. **Fast and purposeful** — animations should take 150–300ms. Nothing over 400ms for UI transitions.\n   311→2. **Spring feels good, ease feels cheap** — use `type: \"spring\"` with `stiffness: 300, damping: 30` for interactive elements.\n   312→3. **Animate layout changes** — use `layout` prop on elements that reorder or resize.\n   313→4. **Reveal, don't decorate** — animations should help the user understand what's happening, not show off.\n   314→\n   315→### Standard configs\n   316→\n   317→```ts\n   318→// Fade in (page section reveal, card appear)\n   319→const fadeIn = {\n   320→  initial: { opacity: 0, y: 8 },\n   321→  animate: { opacity: 1, y: 0 },\n   322→  transition: { duration: 0.2, ease: \"easeOut\" },\n   323→};\n   324→\n   325→// Slide up (bottom sheets, prompts)\n   326→const slideUp = {\n   327→  initial: { opacity: 0, y: 20 },\n   328→  animate: { opacity: 1, y: 0 },\n   329→  exit: { opacity: 0, y: 20 },\n   330→  transition: { type: \"spring\", stiffness: 400, damping: 35 },\n   331→};\n   332→\n   333→// Scale tap (buttons, set confirmation)\n   334→const scaleTap = {\n   335→  whileTap: { scale: 0.97 },\n   336→  transition: { type: \"spring\", stiffness: 500, damping: 30 },\n   337→};\n   338→\n   339→// Stagger children (list of cards, exercise rows)\n   340→const staggerContainer = {\n   341→  animate: { transition: { staggerChildren: 0.04 } },\n   342→};\n   343→const staggerItem = {\n   344→  initial: { opacity: 0, y: 6 },\n   345→  animate: { opacity: 1, y: 0 },\n   346→};\n   347→```\n   348→\n   349→### When to animate\n   350→\n   351→| Element | Animation |\n   352→|---------|-----------|\n   353→| Page/section mount | `fadeIn` (staggered for lists) |\n   354→| Set logged confirmation | Green flash + `scaleTap` on the row |\n   355→| Effort/soreness prompt | `slideUp` with `AnimatePresence` |\n   356→| Session card collapse/expand | `layout` + height transition |\n   357→| Milestone achievement | Burst + `fadeIn` with spring bounce |\n   358→| Modal/dialog | `slideUp` + backdrop `fadeIn` |\n   359→| Sidebar active indicator | `layout` so it slides between items |\n   360→\n   361→---\n   362→\n   363→## 8. Gestalt Principles Applied\n   364→\n   365→### Proximity\n   366→Group related elements tightly and separate unrelated elements with space. In the session tracker:\n   367→- All sets for one exercise: `gap: 4px` between rows\n   368→- Between exercises: `gap: 16px`\n   369→- Between session sections: `gap: 24px`\n   370→\n   371→### Similarity\n   372→Consistent visual treatment for the same type of element across all screens:\n   373→- All \"start action\" buttons use the accent orange\n   374→- All \"completed\" states use the success green + strikethrough\n   375→- All metadata (dates, IDs, branch names) uses `font-mono` + `content-muted`\n   376→\n   377→### Continuity\n   378→The sidebar provides spatial continuity across all pages. The active indicator should animate smoothly between items (use framer-motion `layout` on the highlight).\n   379→\n   380→### Figure/Ground\n   381→Cards on `bg-surface` on top of `bg-base` creates clear figure/ground separation. Never use the same background for a card and its container.\n   382→\n   383→### Closure\n   384→Progress bars should always show a track (even at 0%) so the user understands what \"full\" looks like. Empty stats cards should show the outline of what will be there.\n   385→\n   386→---\n   387→\n   388→## 9. Empty, Loading, and Error States\n   389→\n   390→⛔ Every page and component MUST have all three states designed. Never ship a `Loading...` text string or an empty `null` render.\n   391→\n   392→### Loading\n   393→```tsx\n   394→// Skeleton lines — match the shape of the real content\n   395→<div style={{\n   396→  height: 16, borderRadius: 4,\n   397→  background: \"linear-gradient(90deg, #DDD2BF 25%, #D3C8B5 50%, #DDD2BF 75%)\",\n   398→  backgroundSize: \"200% 100%\",\n   399→  animation: \"shimmer 1.5s infinite\",\n   400→  width: \"60%\",\n   401→}} />\n   402→```\n   403→\n   404→Add the shimmer keyframe to globals.css once and reuse everywhere.\n   405→\n   406→### Empty state\n   407→```tsx\n   408→// Structure: icon + heading + subtext + optional CTA\n   409→<div style={{ textAlign: \"center\", padding: \"48px 24px\" }}>\n   410→  <div style={{ /* icon circle */ }}>\n   411→    <DumbbellIcon size={24} color=\"#988A78\" />\n   412→  </div>\n   413→  <h3>No sessions logged yet</h3>\n   414→  <p>Complete your first session to see it here.</p>\n   415→  <button>Start Session →</button>\n   416→</div>\n   417→```\n   418→\n   419→Empty states should be encouraging, not diagnostic. Write copy that tells the user what to do next, not what's missing.\n   420→\n   421→### Error state\n   422→```tsx\n   423→// Show context-aware message, not a raw error string\n   424→<div style={{\n   425→  background: \"rgba(184,48,32,0.08)\",\n   426→  border: \"1px solid rgba(184,48,32,0.3)\",\n   427→  borderRadius: 8, padding: \"12px 16px\",\n   428→  color: \"#2C1A10\", fontSize: 14,\n   429→}}>\n   430→  <span style={{ color: \"#B83020\", fontWeight: 600 }}>\n   431→    Something went wrong.\n   432→  </span>{\" \"}\n   433→  {friendlyMessage}\n   434→</div>\n   435→```\n   436→\n   437→Never show `error.message` directly to users for auth/network errors. Map known Supabase error codes to friendly messages (see lib/errors.ts — TODO).\n   438→\n   439→---\n   440→\n   441→## 10. Anti-Patterns ⛔\n   442→\n   443→These patterns are explicitly banned. If you see them, fix them.\n   444→\n   445→| Anti-pattern | Why | Instead |\n   446→|---|---|---|\n   447→| `bg-gradient-to-r from-... to-...` as a card background | Looks generic/cheap | Solid surface colors with thoughtful borders |\n   448→| Glassmorphism (`backdrop-blur` + translucent bg) | Bad perf, illegible text | Solid elevated surface |\n   449→| Multiple accent colors in one view | Creates visual noise | One accent, one semantic color |\n   450→| Nested cards inside cards inside cards | Creates mud | Use `Elevated` card variant, or just spacing |\n   451→| `shadow-xl` on everything | Flat design looks stronger | Reserve box-shadow for true floating elements |\n   452→| All-caps body text | Hard to read at length | Use weight/color for hierarchy instead |\n   453→| Placeholder text as the only label | Bad accessibility | Always have a real `<label>` |\n   454→| `onClick={() => router.push(...)}` on a div | Not keyboard accessible | Use `<a>` or `<button>` |\n   455→| `display: flex; justify-content: space-between` for form actions | Breaks on mobile | Stack vertically or use gap |\n   456→| Coach form assessment data exposed in user views | Security violation | Use `getFormBadge()` only |\n   457→| Modifying `lib/roadmap-data.ts` in parallel agent runs | Merge conflicts | Kickoff API manages status |\n   458→\n   459→---\n   460→\n   461→## 11. Page-Level Patterns\n   462→\n   463→### Authenticated app shell\n   464→\n   465→Every page inside `app/(app)/` gets:\n   466→- Sidebar (220px fixed left on `lg+`)\n   467→- Sticky header (mobile only, 56px)\n   468→- Main content area: `px-4 py-6 lg:px-8`\n   469→\n   470→### Form pages (onboarding, settings)\n   471→\n   472→- Max width: `480px` (centered in content area, not full page)\n   473→- Use the `Accent-edge` card variant for the active step\n   474→- Progress indicator at top for multi-step flows\n   475→\n   476→### Data pages (sessions, progress, coach clients)\n   477→\n   478→- Use a sticky subheader for filters/controls\n   479→- Page title + description in a `24px` padded section at top\n   480→- Main content in cards below\n   481→\n   482→### Table/list pages (admin users, exercises)\n   483→\n   484→- Full-width table inside a card\n   485→- Row hover: `bg-hover`\n   486→- Selected row: `accent` left border\n   487→- Actions column: always rightmost, `DropdownMenu` for ≥2 actions\n   488→\n   489→---\n   490→\n   491→## 12. Seed Data & Program Structure\n   492→\n   493→The default 12-week program uses this structure:\n   494→\n   495→**3 Phases × 12 weeks × 3 sessions/week = 36 unique workout templates per program**\n   496→\n   497→```\n   498→Phase 1 — Foundation (Weeks 1–4):  3×12 reps,  learning movements\n   499→Phase 2 — Build      (Weeks 5–8):  4×8  reps,  progressive overload\n   500→Phase 3 — Peak       (Weeks 9–12): 5×5  reps,  peak strength\n   501→\n   502→Session A — Lower body:  Squat, Romanian DL, Leg Press, Lunge, Face Pull\n   503→Session B — Upper push:  Bench Press, Incline DB, Overhead Press, Tricep Pushdown\n   504→Session C — Pull + hinge: Deadlift, Barbell Row, Lat Pulldown, Cable Row, Dips\n   505→```\n   506→\n   507→Weight tiers: `pre_baseline` → `default` → `post_baseline` (low → standard → advanced)\n   508→Gender split: `_f` (female defaults) and `_m` (male defaults) on every template exercise.\n   509→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it looks malicious. If it does, you MUST refuse to improve or augment the code. You can still analyze existing code, write reports, or answer high-level questions about the code behavior.\n</system-reminder>\n"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"a5772f8b-9e1a-462f-a905-3db4d6853979","uuid":"805854d1-b64b-4183-9b24-96318840c141"}
